A credit report is basically a past report of the borrower's credit history from a different variety of resources, such as banks, credit card providers, collection agencies, and state & federal governments. \r\n\r\n💲 Acquiring and understanding credit reports and scores – Fair Credit Reporting Act, Experian, Equifax, TransUnion, etc.\r\nClients can frequently check their credit history by asking for credit reports from credit.\r\nIn the United States, the Fair Credit Reporting Act governs organizations that compile credit reports. These businesses vary from the big three credit reporting agencies, Experian, Equifax, TransUnion, to specialty credit reporting agencies like myFico and others.\r\n     \r\n💲 Credit history of immigrants\r\n\r\nCredit history normally stays inside one country. Even within the same credit card network or within the same international credit bureau, information is not shared between different countries. For example, Equifax Canada never shares any kind of credit information with the Equifax situated in the United States. \r\n\r\n💲 Adverse credit (sub-prime credit)\r\nUnfavorable credit history, also called sub-prime credit history, non-status credit history, impaired credit history, poor credit history, and bad credit history, is a damaging credit score.\r\nThere are many alternatives for people with bad credit, we will teach you how to fix your credit score / repair credit score, and will show you alternative ways to get credit.\r\n\r\n💲 Free annual credit report – 3 bureau credit report\r\n\r\nBecause of the FACT Law  each legitimate U.S. citizen is entitled to a free copy of his or her credit scores report from each credit score reporting bureau once every 12 months.
